the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, the Registrant has duly caused
this Report to be signed on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">LANDEC
CORPORATION REPORTS FIRST QUARTER</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FISCAL
YEAR 2005 RESULTS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">MENLO PARK, CA &#150;
September 28, 2004 &#150; Landec Corporation (Nasdaq: LNDC), a developer and
marketer of technology-based polymer products for food, agricultural and
licensed partner applications, today reported results for the first quarter ended
August 29, 2004.&#160; Unless otherwise noted,
all financial statement amounts are stated on a basis consistent with
accounting principles generally accepted in the United States (&#147;GAAP basis&#148;).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total revenues for the quarter were $46.9 million
versus revenues of $41.8 million for the same period a year ago.&#160; The Company reported a net loss for the
quarter of $692,000 or $0.03 per diluted share compared to a net loss of
$624,000, or $0.03 per diluted share, for the first quarter of fiscal year
2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The results for the prior year first quarter include
revenues and gross profits from the Company&#146;s former domestic commodity
vegetable business which was sold at the end of June 2003.&#160; In the prior year first quarter ended August
31, 2003, revenues and gross profits from selling domestic commodity vegetable
products were $1.6 million and $523,000, respectively.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The results for the first quarter are in line with
achieving our goals of continuing to grow Apio&#146;s technology-based specialty
packaging produce business, while at the same time continuing to reduce
Company-wide operating costs,&#148; commented Gary Steele, President and CEO of
Landec. &#147;Consistent with the seasonality in our business and with the results
from fiscal year 2004, we expect that the first half of fiscal year 2005 should
show losses, and the second half and the full year are expected to be
profitable.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec has achieved the
following key milestones thus far in fiscal year 2005:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apio, Inc., Landec&#146;s Food
Subsidiary:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Entered into a joint technology development and
supply agreement with Chiquita, for Apio to supply its proprietary banana
packaging to Chiquita for sale with Chiquita<font face="Symbol">&#226;</font>
Brand bananas.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increased value-added specialty packaging
vegetable revenues by 13% compared to the same period in the prior year.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increased the sales of the value added vegetable
tray line by 100% and the value-added 12-ounce product line by 10% compared to
the same period in the prior year.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increased export revenues by 40% and export gross
profits by 38% compared to the same period last year.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reduced operating expenses by $371,000 or 10%
compared to the first quarter a year ago.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Established a new $10 million working capital
line of credit and a $6 million equipment line of credit with better terms and
more favorable financial covenants.</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec Ag, Landec&#146;s
Agricultural Seed Subsidiary:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Introduced 26 new corn hybrids for 2005, bringing
the line-up to 116 hybrid seed varieties it currently has for sale.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Included in the 116 hybrid seed varieties are 49
hybrid offerings that will be using Early Plant<sup><font face="Symbol">&#226;</font></sup>
Intellicoat<font face="Symbol">&#226;</font> seed coating technology, up from 32 last year.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec Consolidated:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reduced Company-wide interest expense by $158,000
or 57% compared to the first quarter of fiscal year 2004.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We have five primary objectives for fiscal year
2005:&#160; (1) grow our value-added specialty
packaged food business, (2) grow our ag seed customer base and corresponding
revenues for all of our seed products, (3) commercially launch our banana
packaging technology with Chiquita, (4) continue to add strategic partner
relationships in each of our businesses, and (5) at least double net income
compared to fiscal year 2004 results and increase revenues to over $200
million,&#148; added Steele.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Apio, Inc.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;During the first quarter, sales of our value-added
specialty packaging vegetable products grew 13% to $25.2 million compared to
$22.3 million in the same period last year,&#148; stated Steele.&#160; &#147;Notably, our Eat Smart</font><font face="Symbol">&#226;</font>
12-ounce specialty packaged retail product line grew 10% during the first
quarter compared to the same period last year and our Eat Smart vegetable tray
product line grew 100% compared to the same period last year.&#160; Partially offsetting the sales increases in
vegetable trays and 12-ounce products was a decrease in sales volume of bagged
products to club stores, primarily due to the realignment of distribution
centers by a club store customer that we had previously disclosed.&#160; According to AC Nielsen, for the three months
ended June 30, 2004, Apio was the number one supplier of vegetable party trays
to retail grocery stores in the United States, capturing 37% of the total
retail vegetable party tray market.&#160; This
is an increase of 14 percentage points from 23% for the three months ended June
30, 2003.&#160; This market share data was
based on sales reported for retail grocery stores with average annual revenues
over $2 million that report to AC Nielsen.&#160;
In addition, Apio&#146;s export revenues increased 40% to $17.7 million from
$12.6 million during the first quarter last year and export gross profits
increased 38% to $1.0 million from $751,000 during the same period a year ago.&#148;</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Apio&#146;s first quarter gross profits from value-added
vegetable products decreased $139,000, or 3% compared to the prior year
quarter.&#160; This decrease in gross profits
is primarily due to discontinuing lower margin value-added products in
preparation for introducing new value-added products in the second fiscal
quarter.&#160; The gross margins on the
discontinued products were considerably lower than our average value-added
margins.&#160; In addition, certain packaging
inventory associated with these discontinued products was written off.&#160; The combination of lower gross margins on the
sale of discontinued products and inventory write offs resulted in lower
value-added gross profits at Apio during this year&#146;s first quarter,&#148; said
Steele. &#147;Offsetting the lower value-added gross profits, Apio reduced operating
expenses by $371,000, resulting in net income for Apio during the first quarter
of $1.3 million, an 8% increase compared to the prior year quarter.&#148;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;In our banana program,
we recently announced that Apio has entered into a joint technology development
and supply agreement with Chiquita Brands International, Inc.&#160; Under the terms of the agreement, Apio will
supply Landec&#146;s proprietary Intelimer</font><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#226;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> based packaging to Chiquita.&#160; Chiquita in turn will package Chiquita</font><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#226;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
Brand bananas with Landec&#146;s proprietary banana packaging for sale worldwide,&#148;
stated Steele.&#160; &#147;This agreement with
Chiquita is the culmination of several years of market trials with bananas to
validate our technology and its value in the marketplace.&#160; We are looking forward to working with
Chiquita to commercially launch several packaging formats worldwide using our
proprietary banana packaging.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Landec Consolidated</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The net loss for the
quarter was comparable to the net loss during the first quarter last year due
to several offsetting increases and decreases.&#160;
Items increasing the net loss include: (1) a $582,000 reduction in Apio
service revenue gross profits primarily due to the Company selling its domestic
commodity vegetable business in June 2003, (2) a $139,000 reduction in Apio
value-added gross profits and (3) planned increases in sales and marketing
costs for Apio and Landec Ag of $302,000.&#160;
These increases in the net loss were offset by: (1) a $288,000 increase
in gross profits from Apio&#146;s export business, (2) a $324,000 Company-wide
reduction in general and administrative expenses, (3) a $203,000 decrease in
research and development expenses primarily due to a greater emphasis in the
banana program on sales and marketing, and (4) a $158,000 reduction in interest
expenses,&#148; continued Steele.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Commenting on the
financial condition of the Company, Steele said, &#147;During the first quarter
ended August 29, 2004, we maintained our strong balance sheet.&#160; The cash decrease of $873,000 during the
quarter to a cash balance of $5.6 million was primarily due to (a) net cash
used in operations of $538,000 and (b) the purchase of $889,000 of property,
plant and equipment, partially offset by an increase in net borrowings under
the Company&#146;s lines of credit of $565,000.&#160;
As of August 29, 2004, we had availability under our lines of credit of
$10.5 million.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;As
a reminder about the seasonal nature of our business, seasonality is inherent
in our two core businesses &#150; Apio and Landec Ag.&#160; Apio is subject to produce sourcing issues
during the winter months, and Landec Ag recognizes nearly</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> all of its revenues and profits during
our third and fourth fiscal quarters while realizing essentially no revenues
during our first and second fiscal quarters,&#148; commented Steele.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Landec&#146;s proprietary temperature-activated Intelimer
polymers are patent protected and are changing the economics and the quality of
the food and seed products we have targeted.&#160;
In addition, our technology is opening up new solutions in the medical,
consumer and industrial markets.&#160; We have
numerous technology-driven applications in our pipeline and look forward to
developing several new products with partners during the upcoming year,&#148;
concluded Steele.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Operating Highlights and Outlook</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apio&#146;s
Intelimer Based Packaging Products Business Continues to Grow</font></b></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the past twelve
months, Apio introduced thirty-one new value-added produce product offerings,
including sixteen new Dole branded products.&#160;
Apio currently sells over 120 value-added products to retail, club store
and food service customers.&#160; In addition,
Apio has expanded its retail and club store presence to nearly 10,500 stores.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec&#146;s Intelimer-based food packaging regulates the
levels of oxygen and carbon dioxide within a package to maintain the optimum
atmosphere for the particular vegetable(s) in order to extend the shelf life of
the produce. The success of Landec&#146;s Intelimer-based food packaging technology
allows the Company to convert not only fresh-cut produce but also whole produce
into value-added products that bring real differentiation to retailers and to
growers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first quarter
of fiscal year 2005, Apio continued to grow its value-added business.&#160; Sales from the two fastest-growing product
lines, which consist of vegetable trays and 12-ounce retail packages,
collectively grew over 58% compared to the same period of the prior year.&#160; The Company expects to continue to grow its
market share in its value-added product lines during the remainder of fiscal
year 2005.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec
Ag&#146;s Intellicoat Seed Coating Product Sales Grew this Past Year</font></b></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec Ag, the Company&#146;s Intellicoat seed coating
subsidiary, commercially launched its Early Plant corn during 2003.&#160; Early Plant hybrid corn joined the existing
line-up of Landec Ag commercial products which include Pollinator Plus&#174;
coatings for inbred corn seed, Relay</font><font face="Symbol">&#228;</font>
Cropping System of wheat and Intellicoat coated soybean, Fielder&#146;s Choice
Direct<font face="Symbol">&#226;</font> hybrid corn and the Harvestar<font face="Symbol">&#226;</font>
product line, which offers high performance alfalfa and nutrient enhanced
hybrid corn seed.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Early Plant corn is
designed to allow corn farmers to safely and reliably
plant hybrid corn three to four weeks earlier than normal, by using Landec Ag&#146;s
proprietary Intellicoat coating which prevents germination until the soil
reaches the optimal soil germination temperature.&#160; Otherwise, planting earlier in cold, wet soil
could cause poor or no germination to occur.&#160;
Allowing the farmer to have a wider planting window lowers costs,
reduces risks associated with late planting and potentially increases yields
across the entire farming operation. The program for Early Plant corn increased
40% this past spring to over 56,000 acres from 40,000 acres in the spring of
2003 and over four-fold from 13,000 acres in the spring of 2002.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For Early Plant corn
planted in 2003, the Intellicoat coated seeds showed better, more uniform
emergence and higher stand counts for improved yield potential when compared to
uncoated corn seeds.&#160; Landec Ag&#146;s
commercial launch in 2003 of its Intellicoat Early Plant corn seed coating
technology included its own Fielder&#146;s Choice Direct brand of hybrid seed corn
and the hybrid corn seed brands of three regional seed companies.&#160; Testimonials from farmers for their 2003 crop
indicated that Early Plant corn yielded on average an increase in bushels per
acre compared to corn planted at normal planting times and avoided losses
associated with late planting of corn.&#160;
In addition, seven seed companies commercially tested Intellicoat coated
Early Plant corn under their brand names with key customers to prepare for a
broader launch of Early Plant corn in 2005.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\cmuller\04-11007-1\task190177\11007-1-mm.htm',USER='cmuller',CD='Sep 28 14:39 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec Ag&#146;s first
Intellicoat-based commercial product is called Pollinator Plus.&#160; Pollinator Plus seed coatings are applied to
inbred seed corn to delay seed germination and extend the pollination window
thus reducing risks and increasing yields for seed companies. Pollinator Plus
is being used by 40 major seed companies in the production of hybrid seed corn.&#160; This product line was planted on nearly
74,000 acres in 2004 compared to 66,000 acres in 2003.&#160; In addition, during 2003 Landec Ag entered
into a non-exclusive joint licensing agreement with Incotec International BV, a
recognized world leader in seed coating enhancement technologies, which is
making Pollinator Plus coatings available to the European Union market.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec Ag, headquartered
in Monticello, Indiana, combines its proprietary Intellicoat seed coating
technology products with its unique electronic, direct marketing and
consultative selling approach - eDC&#174;, which is supported by its sophisticated
telephonic and electronic call center. Landec Ag&#146;s information systems provide
its sales force with in-depth information about the customer&#146;s farming trends
and requirements, while also helping the farmer to better evaluate seed choices
in order to match appropriate offerings with the farmer&#146;s specific
requirements.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Landec&#146;s
Intelimer Supply and Licensing Business Continues to Expand</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec began shipping
Intelimer polymers to L&#146;Oreal of Paris in November 2003 for use in cosmetic and
personal care products.&#160; L&#146;Oreal has now
commercialized initial products in Asia, Europe and the United States using
Landec&#146;s Intelimer polymer additives.&#160;
The Company is working with L&#146;Oreal and other companies to expand the
use of Intelimer polymers in other cosmetic and personal care products.&#160; In addition, we have developmental efforts
underway relating to new applications of our Intelimer materials outside of the
food and agricultural markets.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h4 style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec First Quarter 2005 Earnings Conference Call</font></b></h4>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A conference call will follow this release at 8:00
a.m. Pacific Time on Wednesday, September 29, 2004, during which senior
management of Landec will present an overview of results for the first quarter
of fiscal year 2005.&#160; Interested parties
have the opportunity to listen to the conference call live on the Internet at
www.landec.com on the Investor Relations web page.&#160; A replay of the webcast will be available for
30 days.&#160; Additionally investors can
listen to the call by dialing (866) 244-4515 or (703) 639-1168 at least 5
minutes prior to the start.&#160; A replay of
the call will be available through Wednesday, October 6th by calling (888)
266-2081<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">  </font></b>or<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">  </font></b>(703)
925-2533, code #549186.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Landec Corporation designs, develops, manufactures and
sells temperature-activated and other specialty polymer products for a variety
of food, agricultural and licensed partner applications. The Company&#146;s
temperature-activated polymer products are based on its proprietary Intelimer
polymers which differ from other polymers in that they can be customized to
abruptly change their physical characteristics when heated or cooled through a
pre-set temperature switch.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Except for the historical
information contained herein, the matters discussed in this news release are
forward-looking statements that involve certain risks and uncertainties that
could cause actual results to differ materially, including such factors among
others, as the timing and expenses associated with expanding operations, the
ability to achieve acceptance of the Company&#146;s new products in the market
place, weather conditions that can affect the supply and price of produce, the
amount and timing of research and development funding and license fees from the
Company&#146;s collaborative partners, the timing of regulatory approvals and new
product introductions, the mix between pilot production of new products and
full-scale manufacturing of existing products, the mix between domestic and
international sales, and the risk factors listed in the Company&#146;s Form 10-K for
the fiscal year ended May 30, 2004.&#160; (See
item 2: Management&#146;s Discussion and Analysis of Financial Condition and Results
of Operations.)&#160; As a result of these and
other factors, the Company expects to continue to experience significant
fluctuations in quarterly operating results and there can be no assurance that
the Company will remain consistently profitable.&#160; The Company undertakes no obligation to
update or revise any forward-looking statements whether as a result of new
developments or otherwise.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

and Q&amp;A to Follow&#151;</font></b></h5>

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CONSOLIDATED CONDENSED STATEMENTS OF OPERATIONS</font></b></p>

thousands, except per-share data)</font></i></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">LANDEC
CORPORATION</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FIRST
QUARTER ENDED AUGUST 29, 2004</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">QUESTIONS AND ANSWERS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1)&#160; What are the Company&#146;s primary areas of focus
for the remainder of fiscal year 2005?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .2in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">For
the remainder of fiscal year 2005 we intend to focus on the following areas of
operation:</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a.</font></i></b><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Work with Chiquita to rapidly commercialize our
packaging technology for bananas.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">b.</font></i></b><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increase Apio&#146;s value-added revenues from retail
grocery and foodservice by 15% to 20% compared to fiscal year 2004.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">c.</font></i></b><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Expand
Apio&#146;s value-added business through use of its exclusive domestic packaging and
marketing agreement with Dole Fresh Vegetables, Inc.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">d.</font></i></b><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increase
gross profits in Apio&#146;s value-added business by 15% to 20% compared to fiscal
year 2004 by reducing production costs and focusing on higher margin products.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">e.</font></i></b><b><i><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reduce losses in Apio&#146;s
banana program by approximately $1.4 million compared to fiscal year 2004</i></b>
<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">by no longer sourcing bananas and only selling
banana packaging with Intelimer technology to Chiquita and other companies.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">f.</font></i></b><b><i><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Grow Landec Ag&#146;s uncoated
seed revenues by 15% to 20% and its Intellicoat coated seed revenues by 50% or
more and grow overall ag gross profits by 20% or more
compared to fiscal year 2004.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">g.</font></i></b><b><i><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increase product sales to
L&#146;Oreal and others.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">h.</font></i></b><b><i><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Increase fiscal year revenues
to over $200 million, at least double net income compared to fiscal year 2004,
and generate positive cash flow from operations.</i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2) The
recent announcement concerning the joint technology and licensing agreement
with Chiquita elicits the following questions:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What product(s) is the Company selling to
Chiquita under the recently entered into agreement?&#160; What is the sales price?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">We
will be selling our proprietary breathable membranes to Chiquita.&#160; The price for the membranes will vary based
on the size of the membrane.&#160; The price we
are charging per membrane is confidential and will not be disclosed.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Does this agreement change the Company&#146;s
forecast for a loss of $1.0 million in the banana program during fiscal year
2005?&#160; If so, what is the new projected
loss?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">At
this time, given the start up costs and development costs associated with
initiating commercialization, we are still estimating that our loss in the
banana program during fiscal year 2005 will approximate our original estimate
of $1.0 million.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What are the exclusive fields and the
non-exclusive fields covered by this agreement?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">The
exclusive fields are selective and confidential. For competitive and
confidentiality reasons we do not intend to disclose any more details
concerning exclusive versus non-exclusive fields at this time.</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='9',FILE='C:\JMS\cmuller\04-11007-1\task190177\11007-1-mm.htm',USER='cmuller',CD='Sep 28 14:39 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What are the minimums based on and what
are the thresholds to maintain exclusivity?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">The
minimums are based on annual purchases of membranes and increase over
time.&#160; The thresholds are confidential
and will not be disclosed.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What is the term of the agreement?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">The
agreement is a multi-year agreement with an option for Chiquita to extend the
agreement.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What impact will this agreement have on
fiscal year 2006 results?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">It is
very difficult to estimate at this time.&#160;
We should begin selling membranes to Chiquita during the 2<sup>nd</sup>
half of this fiscal year and we won&#146;t know the build up until some time
thereafter.&#160; However, we anticipate that
the banana program should at least breakeven in fiscal year 2006.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">g)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What are the initial packaging formats
and markets that will be targeted?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Because
we entered into this agreement only recently, and the parties are just
beginning to work together as a joint team, it will take some time to determine
the most appropriate initial packaging formats and target markets.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What is the status of the Dole branded
specialty packaging products?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">We
are selling sixteen Dole branded bagged and vegetable tray products to
retailers and club stores.&#160; Sales of Dole
branded products increased during the first quarter of fiscal year 2005
compared to the prior quarter.&#160; In
addition, Dole branded vegetable tray sales have grown significantly since
their introduction last November.&#160;
According to AC Nielsen, for the three months ended June 30, 2004, the
Dole branded vegetable tray was the fifth highest selling retail vegetable tray
in the nation.&#160; We expect the Dole line
of products to solidly contribute to revenues and profits during fiscal year
2005.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What levels of capital and R&amp;D
expenditures are expected in order to grow your core businesses?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">For
fiscal year 2005, we expect capital expenditures of approximately $5 million as
we significantly expand and further automate our food processing capabilities
at Apio. &#160;We expect R&amp;D expenses for
fiscal year 2005 to be less than the $3.7 million spent during fiscal year 2004
as we focus more of our banana efforts on sales and marketing technical support
instead of research and development.</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='10',FILE='C:\JMS\cmuller\04-11007-1\task190177\11007-1-mm.htm',USER='cmuller',CD='Sep 28 14:39 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">What plan does the Company have to
minimize the negative financial impact from winter sourcing issues?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">In
planning for the upcoming winter, the Company is further enhancing the
strategies we started in fiscal year 2004, which include:</font></i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Improving production and
inventory controls</font></i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Obtaining produce sourcing from
geographically dispersed regions</font></i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Developing a system to store
broccoli for a longer period of time before processing</font></i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Diversifying our product mix to
become less reliant on broccoli</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s cash position is $5.6 million at August
29, 2004.&#160; Does the Company have enough
cash resources to continue to operate effectively?</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 19.2pt;text-indent:-19.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">In addition to the $5.6 million in cash, the Company had as
of the end of the first quarter $10.5 million available under its lines of
credit.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Also, during the last two years, the Company has paid down
long-term debt by over 80% to $3.6 million from $17.8 million.&#160; This will reduce our annual principal and
interest payments by approximately $3.7 million.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Furthermore,
the cash to be received by the Company from the purchase by Chiquita of up to
500,000 shares of Common Stock of the Company will amount to approximately $3.5
million which will be used to fund expansion in our food and ag
businesses.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">All of the above, combined with expected cash flow from
operations and lower debt payment, should provide sufficient cash resources to
effectively operate the business for the foreseeable future.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>In what personal care
products are Landec&#146;s Intelimer polymers being used and what are the potential
revenues and gross profits from supplying Intelimer polymers to these types of
products?</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Our
initial products are being used in L&#146;Oreal&#146;s lotion and cream products. The
potential revenues and gross profits depend on (1) the number of products in
which L&#146;Oreal and other companies use our polymers, (2) how rapidly these
products are introduced and (3) their ultimate market acceptance after
introduction.&#160; It is too early to
estimate the possible financial impact from supplying products to L&#146;Oreal and
other companies. To date, personal care revenues have not been material to the
Company&#146;s operating results.&#160; We seek to
expand product sales with L&#146;Oreal and other cosmetic and personal care
companies in the future. </font></i></b>&#160;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">We believe the potential use of our materials in personal
care products such as lotions, creams, color cosmetics, lipsticks and hair care
could be significant over time.</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">a)</font></i></b><b><i><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Apio&#146;s trading business
includes its commission-based commodity export business and its
commission-based buy/sell business.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">b)</font></i></b><b><i><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Subsequent to the sale of the
domestic vegetable business in June 2003, service revenues consist solely of
revenues from Apio Cooling LP.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">c)</font></i></b><b><i><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Included in Other is net interest expenses, non-operating
income/expenses and corporate management fees charged to Apio and Landec Ag by
Corporate.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">d)</font></i></b><b><i><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Virtually all of Landec Ag&#146;s
revenues and profits are realized in the Company&#146;s third and fourth fiscal
quarters.</i></b></p>
